Grammar fem, comp
Meaning tales about the world; legends of the land
Construction loka + akkhāyikā

Example

AN 7.49 dutiyasaññāsuttaṃ
lokacintā

fem. speculation about the world; thoughts about (the origin of) the universe [loka + cintā] ✓

Grammar fem, abstr, comp
Meaning speculation about the world; thoughts about (the origin of) the universe
Construction loka + cintā
Compound chaṭṭhī tappurisa (lokassa + cintā)
Commentary (ANa) lokacintā'ti kena nu kho candimasūriyā katā, kena mahāpathavī, kena mahāsamuddo, kena sattā uppāditā, kena pabbatā, kena ambatālanāḷiker'ādayo'ti evarūpā lokacintā.
Sanskrit loka + cintā

Example

lokadhamma 1

masc. worldly matter; things of the world; vicissitudes of life [loka + dhamma] ✓

Grammar masc, comp
Meaning worldly matter; things of the world; vicissitudes of life
Construction loka + dhamma
Compound kammadhāraya (loka + dhamma)

KHP 5 maṅgalasuttaṃ
lokadhamma 2

masc. worldly phenomenon; common condition; (comm) crumbling character of the five aggregates [loka + dhamma] ✓

Grammar masc, comp
Meaning worldly phenomenon; common condition; (comm) crumbling character of the five aggregates
Construction loka + dhamma
Compound kammadhāraya (loka + dhamma)

Sanskrit lokadharma

Example

Sanskrit lokya + sammata

Example
